## DFC-M47 Live installed-state LibreOffice verification recovery notes

- M47 added `scripts/dfc/office-pdf-libreoffice-live-installed-state-smoke.mjs` and `npm run test:office-pdf-libreoffice-live-installed-state-smoke`.
- The smoke launches dev Electron against live app-managed state and does not pass `--user-data-dir`.
- The smoke rejects external LibreOffice `.svpkg` env vars and external runtime/root injection env vars before launch.
- Live app launch passed; Plugin Management opened; the LibreOffice Office PDF entry was visible.
- Opening Plugin Management and status reads did not start a download.
- The live app-managed LibreOffice runtime was missing, so no existing runtime was reused.
- Per M47 rules, the smoke made exactly one internal `install_official_plugin` attempt. It reached `accepted -> pending -> downloading -> failed` and stopped with sanitized diagnostic `fetch_failed`.
- No repeated download, uninstall, reinstall, external `.svpkg` path injection, external runtime path injection, system LibreOffice, PATH fallback, arbitrary executable path, or renderer-provided executable path was used.
- The missing-runtime DOCX fixture attempt stayed blocked with `conversion_engine_missing`; it did not start a download, did not produce a ready `converted_pdf`, and did not silently fallback to markdown/original/plain text/legacy/system/PATH output.
- Ready installed-state DOCX-to-PDF conversion, valid PDF validation, metadata-only PDF preview, and selected-ref Send Plan authority were not reached in M47 because install failed before runtime activation.
- The live smoke failure diagnostics were hardened after the blocked run so renderer console text is redacted by default, UUIDs are redacted, and only sanitized state classes/operation phases/diagnostic codes should appear in evidence.
- Node ABI rebuild and `vue-tsc` passed; Electron ABI rebuild passed for live launch. Final Node ABI rebuild is required after Electron validation.

## DFC-M47 network-reset rerun recovery notes

- Owner reset the network and authorized one more internal install retry.
- The rerun preserved M47 acquisition boundaries: no external `.svpkg` env vars, no external runtime/root injection, no uninstall/reinstall, no system LibreOffice, no PATH fallback, no arbitrary URL input, and no automatic/startup/background/postinstall/conversion-time download.
- The first rerun launch failed before runtime preflight because the renderer did not mount within the smoke timeout; no runtime preflight, install, or download occurred in that failed launch.
- A diagnostic rerun mounted the app and reached the live Plugin Management / official install operation path.
- The run then failed while polling `enginePluginLifecycle.getInstallOperationStatus` with sanitized terminal diagnostic `install_operation_status_timeout` / DB worker status timeout.
- Because that unguarded operation-status poll is only reached after the missing-runtime branch starts the official `install_official_plugin` operation, the authorized install retry budget was treated as consumed and no further download/install retry was attempted.
- Ready installed-state DOCX-to-PDF conversion, valid PDF validation, metadata-only PDF preview, and selected-ref Send Plan authority remain unverified in live installed-state after the network reset.
- The owner-observed `EPIPE: broken pipe, write` dialog came from an orphaned dev Electron process writing to a closed smoke pipe after interruption. The orphan was terminated, and the live smoke harness now has bounded Electron process-tree cleanup plus sanitized status-timeout evidence.
- Next work should diagnose official install reliability without repeated full package retries, covering both the earlier `fetch_failed` and this rerun's operation-status DB worker timeout.
